 ) railway bhartee board antipisi (RRB NTPC) ke 35 hajaar padon par bhartee ke liye pariksha yojit karegaa
 NTPC Exam Date (RRB NTPC Exam Date) will be released by Railway Recruitment Board (RRB) in the coming days
 railway bhartee board ke varisht adhikari ne enditivi se baatcheet main kaha, ''railway bhartee board abhi paramedical bhartee pariksha yojit karne ja rahaa he
 After paramedical, there will be NTPC, Ministerial and Isolated category and Group d recruitment examination
 railway pariksha kendron ko dhyaan main rakhte hue yah tay karegaa ki kis bhartee ke liye pehle pariksha yojit kii jaae
 He said that there is still time in NTPC examination and Railways will issue notifications as soon as the date of examination is fixed
 bataa den ki railway pehle antipisi pariksha kii taarikh, centre or shift detail jari karegaa
 After which the RRB NTPC Admit Card will be issued 4 days before the exam
 ummidavaar neeche die gaye steps ko folon kar admit card downlod kar paaenge
 - Candidates have to go to the RRB website of their region to download the admit card
 - website par die gaye admit card ke link par clic karnaa hoga
 - On opening a new page, you will have to login by filling in your registration number and date of birth
 - aapaki screen par admit card aa jayega
 - You will be able to download your admit card
 - admit card kaa print out bhi le sakenge
 Let us tell you that Railways is currently preparing for paramedical examination
 railway bhartee board ne paramedical category ke tahat hone vaali bhartee pariksha kii detail jari kar di he
 Candidates can check the exam date, city (RRB Paramedical Exam City) and shift details by visiting the RRB website of their region
 pariksha 19, 20 or 21 july ko yojit kii jaaegi
 At the same time, the Paramedical Recruitment Examination Admit Card (RRB Paramedical Admit Card) can be downloaded 4 days before the examination

 Chhota Rajan was wanted in around 85 cases, ranging from harassment to murder, smuggling and drug trafficking

 daaud 2000 main chota rajan par ek hotel main hamalaa bhi karvaa chukaa he, haalanki rajan hotel ke pratham tal se kudakar naatakeey andaaj main hamale se bachakar bhaag niklaa tha

 Navratri 2019: On the second day of Navratri, the Brahmacharini form of Durga Maa is worshiped
 inako gyaan, tapasya or vairaygy kii devi mana jaataa he
 She is called Brahmacharini due to rigorous practice and being absorbed in Brahman
 vidhyaarthiyon ke liye or tapasviyon ke liye inaki puja bahut hi shubh ou faldaayi hoti he
 It is believed that for those whose moon is weak, worship of Mother Brahmacharini is very favorable
 is baar maa ke duusare swaroop kii upasna 07 april ko kii ja rahi he
 What is the method of worship of Mother Brahmacharini? - Wear yellow or white clothes while worshiping Mother Brahmacharini
 - maa ko safed vasteen arpit karen
 Such as - Misri, Sugar or Panchamrit
 - gyaan or vairaygy kaa koi bhi mantra japa ja saktaa he
 - But for Mother Brahmacharini, chanting "om Ain Namah" is considered the best
 - jaleey aahaar or falahar par vishesh dhyaan dena chahie
 What to do on the day of Navratri so that the moon is strong? - Offer white flowers to the Goddess and offer white things
 - devi ko chaandi kaa ardh chandra bhi arpit karen
 - After this, chant at least 3 garlands of "om Shriman Shraman: Chandramse Namah"
 - ab ardh chandra ko laal dhaage main pirokar gale main dhaaran kar len
 - Your mental illnesses will go away
 duusare din kaa vishesh prasad kya he?- duusare din maa ko shakkar kaa bhoga lagaaein
 - Offer it to all members of the household after offering it
 - sab logon kii aayu main vruddhi hogi
 What to do if the money situation is very bad - Take a watery coconut on any day in Navratri
 - use apni god main rakh len
 - After this, chant "om Dun Durgay Namah" at least 108 times
 - nariyal ko le jaakar behate hue jal main pravaahit kar den
 - All your poverty will be removed
